  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer10513722548067740798">Tara Dupont menyukai Paris dan musim gugur.   <span id="freeText10513722548067740798" style="display:none">Tara Dupont menyukai Paris dan musim gugur. Ia mengira sudah memiliki segalanya dalam hidup… sampai ia bertemu Tatsuya Fujisawa yang susah ditebak dan selalu membangkitkan rasa penasarannya sejak awal.<br /><br />Tatsuya Fujisawa benci Paris dan musim gugur. Ia datang ke Paris untuk mencari orang yang menghancurkan hidupnya. Namun ia tidak menduga akan terpesona pada Tara Dupont, gadis yang cerewet tapi bisa menenangkan jiwa dan pikirannya… juga mengubah dunianya.<br /><br />Tara maupun Tatsuya sama sekali tidak menyadari benang yang menghubungkan mereka dengan masa lalu, adanya rahasia yang menghancurkan segala harapan, perasaan, dan keyakinan. Ketika kebenaran terungkap, tersingkap pula arti putus asa… arti tak berdaya… Kenyataan juga begitu menyakitkan hingga mendorong salah satu dari mereka ingin mengakhiri hidup...<br /><br /><i>Seandainya masih ada harapan - sekecil apa pun - untuk mengubah kenyataan, ia bersedia menggantungkan seluruh hidupnya pada harapan itu...</i></span>

        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>  </div>

<div id="review_70777224" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/70777224" />
    <a title="Ratrichibi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1711404-ratrichibi"><img alt="Ratrichibi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1550414367p2/1711404.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/70777224?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ratrichibi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ratrichibi" href="/user/show/1711404-ratrichibi">Ratrichibi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer70777224" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8713076351171215497">After reading Ilana Tan's first book, "Summer in Seoul", I've been looking forward for her next novels. I like her simple writing style and the plots, which sometimes predictable (well, what do you expect for romance stories?) but still have the pinch on some scenes.<br/>When I read Summer In Seoul, the fanfiction-style was still bold and I couldn't help myself not to be excited about it XD<br/>But this Autumn in Paris gave me a new excitement. The story is more mature if I might say, with a heart-throbbi</span>
  <span id="freeText8713076351171215497" style="display:none">After reading Ilana Tan's first book, "Summer in Seoul", I've been looking forward for her next novels. I like her simple writing style and the plots, which sometimes predictable (well, what do you expect for romance stories?) but still have the pinch on some scenes.<br />When I read Summer In Seoul, the fanfiction-style was still bold and I couldn't help myself not to be excited about it XD<br />But this Autumn in Paris gave me a new excitement. The story is more mature if I might say, with a heart-throbbing characters and storyline. That's why I just couldn't get off of this book until the very last page. And even though it's pretty much predictable, but still, love story is not always as cheesy-weasy-lovey-dovey as people thought.<br />Yes, I cried when I read the last 2/3 part of the book &gt;__&lt;<br /><br />I always love the warm feeling in my heart after reading such a good love story :)<br /><br />My favorite quote from this book : <br />"<i>Kalau dia bahagia, aku juga merasa bahagia. Sesederhana itu.</i>"<br /><br />Buku karya Ilana Tan ini mengisahkan tentang Tara Dupont, gadis keturunan Indonesia-Perancis yang tinggal di Paris dan Tatsuya Fujisawa, seorang arsitek dari Jepang.<br /><br />Tara adalah seorang gadis yang memiliki kepribadian menarik. cerewet, ceplas ceplos, namun tulus dan penuh antusiasme. Sedangkan Tatsuya adalah seorang pria pendiam yang membenci musim gugur. Ia juga membenci Paris, namun ia datang ke kota itu untuk menelusuri jejak masa lalunya yang tak terduga sampai ia bertemu dengan Tara. Gadis itu telah mengubah pandangannya tentang dunia, dan memberikan rasa nyaman di hati Tatsuya. Pertemuan-pertemuan mereka di Paris telah menanamkan kesan di hati mereka masing-masing, namun mereka juga harus bergulat dengan luapan masa lalu yang tak terduga.<br /><br />Walaupun kisah cinta cenderung klise, namun kisah Tara dan Tatsuya tetap memberikan rasa penasaran dan kejutan hingga ke akhir cerita. Dengan gaya bahasa yang sederhana dan alur yang mudah dicerna, menjadikan buku Autumn in Paris ini sangat menarik untuk menjadi teman membaca kita di sore hari. Kisah roman manusia urban masa kini dikemas apik dalam buku yang merupakan salah satu bagian dari trilogi musim karya Ilana Tan lainnya, yaitu Summer in Seoul dan Winter in Tokyo. Penggambaran adegan dan karakter yang kuat dari buku ini menjadikan kisah cinta Tara dan Tatsuya lebih menyentuh hati para pembacanya.<br /><br />Buku ini memberikan gambaran tentang kehidupan dan kisah cinta yang kompleks, penuh dengan harapan dan keyakinan yang menepiskan keputusasaan. Memang, tidak semua kisah cinta harus manis, namun tidak semua kisah cinta juga harus menjadi getir, bukan? Menjalani kehidupan mereka yang penuh dengan kejutan dari sejarah hidup masing-masing, penulis buku ini menginspirasikan kita untuk menghadapi kenyataan hidup dengan cinta dan harapan. <br /><br />-chib-</span>
  <a data-text-id="8713076351171215497" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16659222088642959265">So this is the first novel of Ilana Tan that i read, and this did not disappoint me. It has a simple and unique plot, so i never felt bored when i read this. And uh oh, i cried when I was reading some last parts of this book. And I'm in love with the characters <3<br/><br/>Okay, so I'll start the review. and actually this is a very-late-review because i read this book like longtime ago (?), and i write it today, and i don't really remember the plot of the book, so i'm sorry, can't tell you much here.<br/>Here </span>
  <span id="freeText16659222088642959265" style="display:none">So this is the first novel of Ilana Tan that i read, and this did not disappoint me. It has a simple and unique plot, so i never felt bored when i read this. And uh oh, i cried when I was reading some last parts of this book. And I'm in love with the characters &lt;3<br /><br />Okay, so I'll start the review. and actually this is a very-late-review because i read this book like longtime ago (?), and i write it today, and i don't really remember the plot of the book, so i'm sorry, can't tell you much here.<br />Here you go:<br /><br />Kisah cinta tentang gadis cerewet dan pria yang benar-benar susah ditebak. Sifat mereka yang benar-benar bertolak belakang, gadis yang ceria dan pria yang pendiam. Gadis yang sangat menyukai musim gugur dan pria yang membenci musim gugur. Tara Dupont dan Tatsuya Fujisawa memang sudah ditakdirkan untuk bertemu. Namun, ditakdirkan untuk bertemu itu bukan berarti ditakdirkan untuk bersama meskipun saling mencintai, kan? Kisah cinta antara dua orang yang saling mencintai dengan tulus, tetapi kondisi dan masa lalu tak memungkinkan mereka untuk bersama.<br /><br />Aku suka cara penulisnya menuangkan idenya. Kondisinya bisa dibayangkan, ceritanya terasa nyata. Endingnya gak terduga. Novel yang bikin aku nangis. Alurnya bener-bener bagus dan gak pasaran, unik dan gak ngebosenin. Menceritakan kisah cinta yang tulus dan rela berkorban. Wajib dibaca deh bagi yang belom baca, bener-bener unpredictable. Sekian lah hehe. 5 stars pokoknya :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="16659222088642959265" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_903375473" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria Kristina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria Kristina" href="/user/show/13347315-maria-kristina">Maria Kristina</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer903375473" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17931981046193145126">After reading Ilana Tan's Summer in Seoul, I've been looking forward for her next book which is Autumn in Paris.<br/>When I read Summer in Seoul the "happy story" was still stay in my mind, and I so excited about it! :)<br/>Autumn in Paris gave me a really different style of story. Cerita yg lebih matang dan lebih serius tentang masalah tokoh. Autumn in Paris can't make me stop before I finished this book until last page (seriously) and make me cried hard.. huhuhuhu..<br/>The story was unpredictable..<br/>I have fa</span>
  <span id="freeText17931981046193145126" style="display:none">After reading Ilana Tan's Summer in Seoul, I've been looking forward for her next book which is Autumn in Paris.<br />When I read Summer in Seoul the "happy story" was still stay in my mind, and I so excited about it! :)<br />Autumn in Paris gave me a really different style of story. Cerita yg lebih matang dan lebih serius tentang masalah tokoh. Autumn in Paris can't make me stop before I finished this book until last page (seriously) and make me cried hard.. huhuhuhu..<br />The story was unpredictable..<br />I have favorite quote in this book : "Kalau dia bahagia, aku juga merasa bahagia. Sesederhana itu."<br /><br />Buku ini menceritakan tentang Tara dan Tatsuya di kota Paris yg sedang musim gugur (I love autumn.. hehehehe). Tara yang enerjik, periang, penuh antusiasme dan pecinta musim gugur. Tatsuya yang pendiam dan pembenci musim gugur. Keduanya bertemu di Paris dan singkatnya mereka saling jatuh cinta. Tara bisa membawa keceriaan yang membuat hidup Tatsuya lebih berwarna dan Tatsuya bisa memberikan kehangatan yang Tara cari dari seorang pria. <br /><br />Membaca buku ini berarti harus siap emosinya diaduk-aduk dari sweet, happy, love, hope, reality, and than cry.. jujur sampai akhir pun saya pengennya tara dan tatsuya be happy together. tapi kenyataannya lain.. tatsuya memutuskan untuk tidak walking with tara.. he just can't. <br /><br />mengemas semua dengan apik.. kumpulan2 percakapan dengan menggunakan kata2 sederhana yang mengena. semuanya ini ditutup dengan epilog yang cukup manis.<br /></span>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1144420953" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17940754858265975324">So I read this book on 2014 which means last year. I'm re-reading this book as a school assignment, and I was more than thrilled to read this book all over again. I started to forget some parts of the book and to know if my favorite parts of the book are still my favorite parts. The answer is yes.<br/><br/>This book tells a story about a girl and a boy who find love in an unfortunate events in life. This story has an amazing plot line. I remember reading this book for the first time without having any ide</span>
  <span id="freeText17940754858265975324" style="display:none">So I read this book on 2014 which means last year. I'm re-reading this book as a school assignment, and I was more than thrilled to read this book all over again. I started to forget some parts of the book and to know if my favorite parts of the book are still my favorite parts. The answer is yes.<br /><br />This book tells a story about a girl and a boy who find love in an unfortunate events in life. This story has an amazing plot line. I remember reading this book for the first time without having any idea about what this book is about. I thought this book is just another cliche story about two people who fall in love but I was wrong. I FREAKING LOVE THE TWIST!<br /><br />I don't really picture Tatsuya that well in my head, because I never found that person that fits Tatsuya well in my head. But I really love Tatsuya; I love how calm, sweet and caring he is!<br /><br />Tara for me is a jolly girl which I can relate to perfectly! Overall, the characters are amazing.<br /><br />I re-read this book from 5pm and finished it at 10.30pm. That's a record! But this book is really easy and really light (not really, it has a dark ending to it) book to read.<br /><br />For those of you who wants to read a book with a sad ending, this is the book for you.<br /><br />Overall, I'm giving this book a 5/5 stars! I'm not being generous whatsoever, it's because I really love this book and I enjoy it so much. It's the kind of book that you don't want to put down once you pick it up. Highly recommended!</span>

He chose not to contact his dad right away, and somehow the universe led her to meet Tara on many occasions, as if she was the one meant for him. When she started to reciprocate his feelings, he somehow had the guts to call his real-dad? After being blown by the reality, unfortunately, the writer then decided to kill Tatsuya as if to made it easier for them (or Tara) to live and moved on from each other.<br /><br />Don't get me wrong, this is still an enjoyable read. I just pity Tatsuya.<br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YZzMGKNIc+4pA1SQ+zkWOl23TVshdncGlMHiI+IuWA4C65h7iITeqahxD/5g0Hs9qQK4KFtFriX5FGFmXoMe/Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LEL7OEkSV+aBoRR/1xA3KbDB04KCdFmXmsyillsK+ltPNa9bYt76oQDTTxFM+VouRHQm8fhHgLT3GSHT56e8qA==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer12774566011375226051">Ilana Tan adalah seorang novelis Indonesia yang dikenal karena menulis 4 novel roman yang masing-masing novelnya disajikan dengan cerita yang latarnya berbeda-beda. Novel Ilana Tan memiliki keunikan, yaitu tokoh-tokoh dari novel yang satu dengan novel yang lainnya saling berkaitan.[1]<br/>Novel pertamanya berjudul Summer in Seoul, novel keduanya berjudul Autumn in Paris, novel ketiganya berjudul Winter</span>
  <span id="freeText12774566011375226051" style="display:none">Ilana Tan adalah seorang novelis Indonesia yang dikenal karena menulis 4 novel roman yang masing-masing novelnya disajikan dengan cerita yang latarnya berbeda-beda. Novel Ilana Tan memiliki keunikan, yaitu tokoh-tokoh dari novel yang satu dengan novel yang lainnya saling berkaitan.[1]<br />Novel pertamanya berjudul Summer in Seoul, novel keduanya berjudul Autumn in Paris, novel ketiganya berjudul Winter in Tokyo dan novel keempatnya berjudul Spring in London. Masing-masing novel diceritakan di kota-kota besar di dunia, yaitu Seoul (Korea Selatan), Paris (Perancis), Tokyo (Jepang), dan London (Inggris). Dan masing-masing novel diceritakan di musim yang berbeda; Summer (musim panas), Autumn (musim gugur), Winter (musim dingin), dan Spring (musim semi).</span>
  <a data-text-id="12774566011375226051" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
